ANALYSIS    Hauser Feshbach, optical model                        20019  1   62 
            The experimental elastic scattering are compared with 20019  1   63 
            the sum of the calculations of compound elastic and   20019  1   64 
            shape-elastic contributions.  The former is calculated20019  1   65

            fluctuation corrections according to Moldauer.  The   20019  1   67
